    <form n="infl">       
                     <orth orig="Ba" lang="ar">عَمَلَ</orth>
                  </form>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">عَمَلٌ</foreign>, (S, O, Msb, K,) <hi rend="ital">He worked,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">wrought; laboured; served,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">did service: he did, acted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">performed:</hi> (K, TA:) [generally, <hi rend="ital">he did,</hi> &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">with a sort of difficulty,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">with intention;</hi> but sometimes said of an inanimate thing: (see <foreign lang="ar">عَمَلٌ</foreign>, below:)] <hi rend="ital">he did,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">he made, wrought, manufactured,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">constructed,</hi> a thing. (Msb. [See, again, <foreign lang="ar">عَمَلٌ</foreign>, below.]) Accord. to Az, <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَ</foreign> is the only trans. verb of its measure having the inf. n. of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَعَلٌ</foreign>, except <foreign lang="ar">هَبِلَت</foreign>, said of a mother, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">هَبَلٌ</foreign>; other similar verbs having the inf. n. of the measure <foreign lang="ar">فَعْلٌ</foreign>; as <foreign lang="ar">سَرِطْتُ اللُّقْمَةَ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">سَرْطٌ</foreign>; and <foreign lang="ar">بَلِعْتُهُ</foreign>, inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">بَلْعٌ</foreign>. (TA. [But see arts. <foreign lang="ar">سرط</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">بلع</foreign>; with respect to the former of which I must here state that, since it was printed, I have found an authority for <foreign lang="ar">سَرْطٌ</foreign> as inf. n. of <foreign lang="ar">سَرِطَ</foreign> in a copy of the S; though in the K it is said to be <foreign lang="ar">مُحَرَّكَة</foreign>, and accord. to the Msb it is like <foreign lang="ar">تَعَبٌ</foreign>.]) You say, <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلْتُ عَلَى الصَّدَقَةِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">I officiated in the collecting of the poor-rate.</hi> (Msb.) [And <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَ بِمَا فِى كِتَابِ ٱللّٰهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">He did according to what is</hi> enjoined <hi rend="ital">in the Book of God.</hi>] And <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَ فِى هَلَاكِهِ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He laboured to destroy him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">to kill him</hi>]. (K in art. <foreign lang="ar">شيط</foreign>.) [And <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَ فِيهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">It acted upon him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it:</hi> and, said of a sword &amp;c., <hi rend="ital">it had effect,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">made an impression, upon him,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">it.</hi>]          <sense type="b" n="2">-b2-</sense>  [Hence,] <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَ فِيهِ</foreign> signifies [also <assumedtropical>(assumed tropical:)</assumedtropical>  <hi rend="ital">It governed it syntactically;</hi> or <hi rend="ital">caused</hi> it to be <foreign lang="ar">مَرْفُوع</foreign> or <foreign lang="ar">مَنْصُوب</foreign> or <foreign lang="ar">مَجْرُور</foreign> &amp;c.; i. e.] <hi rend="ital">it produced in it a certain species of syntactical desinence.</hi> (K.)          <sense type="b" n="3">-b3-</sense>  And <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَ البَرْقُ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">The lightning was continual.</hi> (K.) And <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَتْ بِأُذُنَيْهَا</foreign>, said of a she-camel, (K,) and also, in a trad., of [the beast] <foreign lang="ar">البُرَاق</foreign>, (O, * TA,) <hi rend="ital">She went quickly,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">swiftly;</hi> (O, K, TA;) because she that does thus puts her ears in motion by reason of the vehemence of the pace. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">عَمِلَت</foreign> [alone] said of a she-camel, signifies [the same: or] <hi rend="ital">She was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, brisk, light, active,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">quick.</hi> (K.)          <sense type="b" n="4">-b4-</sense>  And [hence, app.,] <foreign lang="ar">لَمْ أَرَ النَّفَقَةَ تَعْمَلُ كَمَا تَعْمَلُ بِمَكَّةَ</foreign>, a saying mentioned by Lh, is expl. by ISd as meaning <foreign lang="ar">تَنْفَقُ</foreign> [i. e. <hi rend="ital">I have not seen the money that that one expends pass away as it passes away in Mekkeh</hi>].
